 KILKERRAN OLD CEMETERY Recorded by David and Florence McEwan1984Typed by Ann Boulton, 2006 to 2007(FROM BOTTOM OF CEMETERY ALONG THE … TOP ENTRANCE AND REMNANT WITH URN ON TOP OF MAIN STONE GATE1.	Railed enclosure.  Inscribed stoneErected by AGNES McNAIR relict of the late JOHN RALSTON, merchant in Campbeltown, in memory of JAMES RALSTON their son late merchant in Paisley who died at Campbeltown on the 16th day of March 1841 in the thirty third year of his age.  AGNES RALSTON died on the 3rd Feby 1870 in the 85th year of her age, DAVID RALSTON, merchant Campbeltown and JACKIE RALSTON his wife in memory of their two children both named ROBERT who died in infancy, DAVID RALSTON died July 18 ?.. in the lst year of his age, the above JACKIE RALSTON died 28 December 1891 aged 82 years.  In loving memory of JAMES RALSTON late merchant Montreal, Canada, died January 1886.2.	Railed enclosure.  Polished granite monument surmounted with urnSacred to the memory of CATHERINE CAMPBELL LOVE wife of NEIL McEACHRAN, merchant Glasgow, born 16 Novr 1829, died 13th April 18543.	Walled enclosure.  Inscribed stoneErected in memory of ROBERT RALSTON, merchant, Campbeltown who died 17 May 1840 aged 63, MARGARET DUNLOP his wife died July 1852 aged 72.  ALEXANDER, their son died July 1837 aged 28.  MARGARET their daughter died April 1850 aged 49 also ROBERT, ARCHIEBALD, ELIZABETH and ISABELLA who died in infancy.  JAMES died in Australia in March 1881, ROBERT died in Australia in March 1885, ARCHIEBALD died in Campbeltown in March 1889.4.	Inscribed stoneErected by WILLIAM BREAKENRIDGE in memory of MARY CLARK his spouse who died 3rd March 1812 aged 39 years.  The above WILLIAM BREAKENRIDGE died 31st Dec 1857 aged 85 years, JANET their daughter died 3rd Decr 1880 aged 76 years.5.	Inscribed stoneErected by MATTHEW BREAKENRIDGE in memory of his wife AGNES RALSTON who died 2nd March 1871 aged 55 years and his daughter MARY who died in infancy.  MATTHEW BREAKENRIDGE died 10th Jany 1894 aged 88 years, MARY his daughter who died 2 April 1914 aged 62 years.  JAMES BREAKENRIDGE died 9th July 1927 aged 78 years.6.	Walled enclosure.  Tablet in wall1821.  In memory of JOHN LOVE late Officer of Customs, Campbeltown and CATHERINE STEWART his spouse by MALCOLM McMILLAN their son in law also JOHN and ISABELLA McMILLAN his children who died young.Erected by MALCOLM McMILLAN and MARION McKINNON his wife in memory of their children.  MARY died Jany 28th 1867 aged 2 years, DUNCAN died Sept 27th 187.? Aged 7 years, DONALD died Aug 18th 1878 aged 4 months.7.	Railed enclosure.  Tablets set in wall7.1	In memory of MATTHEW MITCHELL late merchant in Campbeltown 1817.7.2	In memory of MARGARET MITCHELL, widow of Capt. JOHN HUTCHESON died 17th October 18 .. aged 79 years. ENTRANCE GATE8.	Three tablets set in wall within railed enclosure8.1	Sacred to the memory of GRACE CAMPBELL daughter of COLIN CAMPBELL of Auchacrossan died the 4th day of Sept 1853 aged 59 years.8.2	In memory of COLIN CAMPBELL of Auchacrossan who died tenth May MDCCCXIV aged eighty five and of GRACE CAMPBELL his spouse who died seventeenth July MDCCCXXII aged sixty five and of their son Lieut. ROBERT CAMPBELL of the ninety first foot who died thirtieth March MDCCCXXI aged thirty one and also of ANN CAMPBELL sister to the deceased COLIN CAMPBELL who died twenty sixth May MDCCCXV aged eighty seven years.8.3	Sacred to the memory of ANN CAMPBELL daughter of COLIN CAMPBELL of Auchacrossan who died the 9th day of Sepr 1861 aged 74 years.9.	Railed enclosure. Three monuments9.1	By JOHN GRANT, Campbeltown and ISABELLA MACTAGGART, his wife, in memory of their children ANN MACDONALD born 17th Nov 1827, died 29th Dec 1828, ISABELLA born 4th June 1829, died 9th April 1831, LEWIS born 20th April 1833, died 25th Dec. 1846, JOHN GRANT born 22 Oct 1796 died 30 Jan 1849, ISABELLA MACTAGGART born 15th March 1789, died 16th July 1851.9.2	In memory of MARTHA COLVILLE daughter of JOHN COLVILLE jnr Banker and the gentle and beloved wife of JOHN MACTAGGART GRANT,  4 Stonebridge Park, Willesden, London, born at Campbeltown 26th April 1831, died at Willesden 28th June 1910 cremated at Golders Green London N.W.  JOHN MACTAGGART GRANT died 4th March 1924 aged 92 years.9.3	By ALEXANDER ROSS & HELEN  KENNEDY GRANT in memory of their children JOHN GRANT ROSS born 7th June 1863 died 24th January 1865 and ISABELLA ROSS born 14th October 1850 died 13th May 1865, HELEN GRANT ROSS born 15th November 1853 died 27th December 1881.  ALEXANDER ROSS died 4th August 1896 aged 83 years.  HELEN KENNEDY GRANT died 10th March 1905 aged 78 years.10.	Railed enclosure.  Inscribed stone1831	By WILLIAM HARVEY shoemaker, in memory of four of his children who died in infancy.11.	Walled enclosure.  Tablet in wall.Erected by DUNCAN McNAB minister of the Free Church, Campbeltown, in memory of his mother MARY McFARLANE who died 3rd April 1844 aged 56 years and of his three infant sons.  Here lies also his sister JESSIE McNAB who died 30th October 1899 aged 76.12.	Railed enclosure.  Three inscribed stones12.1	In memory of ALAN ANDERSON, Officer of the Fishery, who died 3rd July 1831 aged 66 years and JANET FERGUSON his wife who died 10th Aug 1844 aged 62 years also of their family JOHN died 28th Jan 1813 aged 4½ years, ALEXANDER WILLISON died 27th Oct 1828 aged 18 years, GEORGE died 2nd Feb 1839 aged 23 years, CHARLES HUGH died 3rd Dec 1841 aged 30 years, PATRICK MURRAY died in Trinidad, West Indies 16th March 1845 aged 27 years, by their son JOHN ANDERSON, merchant, Campbeltown.12.2	In affectionate remembrance of JOHN ANDERSON, merchant Campbeltown, who died May1871 aged 57 years12.3	In affectionate remembrance of ELIZABETH ANDERSON born 2nd July 1816 died 16th April 1898.  CHRISTIANA BELL her cousin died 9th October 1906 aged 80 years.13.	Railed enclosure.  Polished granite tablet.This stone sacred to the memory of Capt. WM BENNET MACMILLAN of the Royal Marines who died 24th Feb 1817 aged 36 years, erected by his disconsolate widow KATHERINE MACMILLAN also her daughter MARTHA HAY who died 2nd Nov 1834 aged 22 years and KATHERINE CAMPBELL relict of Capt. W.B. MACMILLAN who died at Geelong, Australia 23rd Sept 1853.14.	Railed enclosure.  Stone tabletErected by filial affection to the memory of Sheriff DUNCAN CAMPBELL who held the situation of Substitute of Kintyre from 1790 to 1822 also to the memory of ANNE, his wife who departed this life in June 1829, DONALD MACMILLAN Esqr. (late of Lephenstrath) died 14th Jan 1864 aged 84 years and his wife ANNE CAMPBELL died 30th Dec 1863 aged 76 years, their son DUGALD CAMPBELL MACMILLAN born 1830 died 1866.15.	Railed enclosure.  Three tablets in wall and one inscribed stone15.1	Erected to the memory of JANET CAMPBELL who died lst April 1852 aged 67 by her husband NATHANIEL HARVEY  “I am the Resurrection and the Life”.15.2	Erected to the memory of MARIA B. LACY who died 7th July 1839 aged 22 years by her husband GEORGE GRAHAM HARVEY.  GEORGE GRAHAM HARVEY died 9th June 1852 aged 44 years.15.3	Erected to the memory of NATHANIEL HARVEY who died 22nd June 1858 aged 81 years.  1st Corinthians 15-48.15.4	In loving memory of ANNIE infant daughter of THOMAS LLOYD HARVEY and EMILY FRANCES his wife born December 5, 1885 died December 6 188515.5	In memory of JANET MUNRO who died the 9th May 1803 aged 23 years.  Erected by NATHL HARVEY, merch. Campbeltown, her husband.16.	Railed enclosure.  Two tablets16.1	In memory of COLIN MATHESON, writer, Campbeltown, who died 29th Dec 1848 aged 76 years and his wife MARY CAMPBELL who died 28th Dec 1848 also their family KENNETH died 26th Feb 1854 aged 50 years, DUNCAN died in Australia Oct 1879, ANNE died 27th Nov 1879 aged 83 years.16.2	Sacred to the memory of HELEN daughter of ALEXANDER WICHTON, merchant, Glasgow, died 13th Oct 1810.17.	Railed enclosureErected to the memory of Captain HENRY BEATSON who died 28 May 1814 aged 70 years also BAZILL HAMILTON his wife who died 23 Nov 1816 aged 58 years, Captain HENRY DUNDAS BEATSON died 4 Sept 1849 aged 65 years, his wife MARGARET STEWART died 23 Oct 1844 aged 55 years, ELIZABETH FULLARTON their daughter died 26 Sep 1841 aged 21 years, ROBERT WILLIAM HAY their son died May 1824 aged 2 years also their son Surgeon General GEORGE STEWART BEATSON, C.B. Honorary Physician to the Queen died at Simla 7 June 1871 aged 60 years, their daughter JANE STEWART BEATSON died at Glasgow 3 Feb 1881 aged 71 years, their son Major General ROGER STEWART BEATSON Royal Engineers died at Bedford Sep 1898 aged 83.18.	CrossHAMILTON BEATSON McMILLAN died 7 Dec 1868 aged 21 erected by his maternal aunts in memory of their beloved nephew.19.	Three tablets19.1	In affectionate remembrance of Surgeon General JOHN FULLARTON BEATSON M.D., C.I.E. fourth son of Capt. H. D. BEATSON who died in London 29 July 1898 in his 81st year and is interred in Paddington Cemetery.19.2	BASIL HAMILTON BEATSON the beloved wife of ALEXANDER McMILLAN W.S. died 25 Oct 1847 aged 31 MARY MACKINNON died 23 Apr 1862 aged 80 years.  She was a faithful servant and friend in the family of Capt. H.D. BEATSON for upwards of 50 years and by her own desire rests here.19.3	CLAUDE GORDON BEATSON 13 Jan 1894 14 Oct 197420.	Railed enclosure.  Two tablets20.1	Erected to the memory of the children of COLIN MACLARTY Esq., of Kilcolmkill and E.S. BREON his wife, MARGARET ELIZABETH died 4 Sep 1808 aged 1 year, COLIN died 8 Jul 1809 aged 3 years, ALEXANDER died 3 Jul 1811 aged 9 years, EDMOND BREON died 19 Feb 1814 aged 10 years also in memory of CHRISTIANA SUSANAH BREON aunt of Mrs COLIN MACLARTY who died 25 Jun 1822 aged 77 years.20.2	Sacred to the memory of GEORGE FRANCIS MACLAVERTY son of J. F. MACLAVERTY Esq., of Keill who died 21 Sep 1852 aged 5 months  and of JOHN FREEMAN MACLAVERTY Esq aged 75 years and of LOUISA his eldest daughter who died 20 Aug 1895 aged 52 years, GRAEME ALEXANDER MACLAVERTY aged 77 years died Oct 26 1923 son of JOHN FREEMAN MACLAVERTY of Keill and of his wife ANNA ELIZA LOCKHART MACLAVERTY who died 15 Apr 1944 at Southport aged 87 years and is buried at Birkdale.21.	Railed enclosure with three inscribed stones.21.1	In memory of Captain THOMAS LACY, H.M.R.C. Hardwicke, who died 1 Apr 1829 aged 58 years and KATHERINE BEATSON his wife who died 1 Mar 1855 aged 74 years also of their family SYDNEY YORKE LACY died 25 Apr 1843 aged 29 years, JOHN LACY died 22 Sep 1843 aged 24 years, JAMES HAMILTON LACY died 30 Jul 1847 aged 24 years, HAMILTON BRISTOW LACY died 25 Sep 1850 aged 39 years, NORMAN McLEOD LACY died and was buried at sea on 13 Jan 1856 on his passage from China to Britain aged 30 years.21.2	In memory of HENRY BEATSON LACY who died 26 Sep 1871 aged 51 years21.3	1850.  To the memory of Captain JAMES MELVILLE, commander of H.M. Revenue Cruiser Wellington, who died 2 Apr 1850 aged 75 years.22.	Inscribed stone1847.  Sacred to the memory of Lieut. ROBERT McGREGOR, Argyle Militia, who died 7 Aug 1847.23.	Railed enclosure1854.  Sacred to the memory of The Revd JOHN CARMICHAEL A.M. for nine years one of the ministers of Campbeltown.  Born at Glasgow 4 Mar 1804, died at Campbeltown 26 May 1853, distinguished by warm affection in the closer relations of life.  He was also an attached and faithful friend.  Easy of access and amiable in manners.  As a pastor he was diligent and devout.  As a preacher fervent and sincere.  As a scholar and divine accomplished and eminent.  This monument was placed over his remains by his people and friends to record their estimation of his public and private character.  “The memory of the just is blessed”. TURN LEFT ALONG BACK WALL24.	Inscribed stone1852	In memory of HUGH GOOLD for many years land steward to his grace the Duke of Argyll who died 3 Nov 1851 aged 66 years, GRACE NEWBIGGING his wife who died 11 Feb 1845 aged ..? years, WILLIAM their youngest son who died 20 Aug 1836 aged 14 years.25.	Inscribed stoneErected by ALEXANDER CAMPBELL in memory of GRACE GOOLD his wife who died at Lochorodale 22 Aug 1864 aged 44 years, ARCHIEBALD their son died 19 Apr 1852 aged 4½ years, ALEXANDER CAMPBELL died at Campbell, North Dakota, 7 Jan 1905 in his 90th year.26.	Walled enclosureSacred to the memory of JOHN FLEMING Esq., of Muasdale, Captain Royal Navy.  He was distinguished in his profession and exemplary in all the duties and relations of life having a good hope through grace of that better life which is eternal in the heavens, he died 23 Apr 1849 aged 76 years.  “The just shall live by faith”.  Rom. 1.17.  27.	Walled enclosure with three tablets27.1	In memory of JAMES BROWN, Surgeon, Argyle and Bute Militia, born March 1771 died 14 June 1855, JANE CAMPBELL his wife who died 10 Feb 1852 and their sons JAMES BROWN Jnr. student born 16 Dec 1802 died 19 Feb 1824, DUGALD CAMPBELL BROWN surgeon born 4 Apr 1801 died 14 Sep 1828 also their old and faithful servant KATHERINE McEACHEN.27.2	Sacred to the memory of ROBERT THOMSON STUART late Lieut. in H.M. 28th Regiment of Foot who died 28 Jan 1870 in his 81st year and his wife HARRIET CAMPBELL who died 26 Jul 1880 in her 89th year, also their daughter JESSIE STUART died 10 Mar 1809 in her 81st year.27.3	In affectionate remembrance of DUGALD ANLEY (widow of the late FERDINAND ANLEY Esq., and dearly beloved mother of Mrs DANIEL TUPPER) who died 10 Mar 1874 aged 75 years also of their mother MARY (widow of Capt. JOHN CAMPBELL younger of Carradale, formerly commander of His Majesty’s Revenue Cruiser Prince of Wales) who died in Feb 1826 also of JANE DOUGLAS CAMPBELL their daughter who died in 1860 all of whom are buried here.  “Blessed are the pure in heart for they shall see God”.28.	Stone obelisk.  Inscriptions vanished TOP ENTRANCE GATE29.	Inscribed stone.To the memory of ANN STEWART wife of THOMAS YOUNG died 5 Nov 182030.	Walled enclosure.Erected to the memory of CHARLES CAMPBELL Esq., late captain in the 79th Regiment of Foot who died in Glasgow 6 Apr 1836 in the 61st year of his age.  He lived respected and he died regretted by all who knew him.  “Take comfort Christians when your friends in Jesus fall asleep …” and ISABELLA HOOK his wife who died 29 Dec 1841 aged 61 years.31.	Stone tablet in walled enclosure.  Inscription very faint.Erected by Capt. CHARLES McALESTER of Philadelphia in memory of his sister ISABELL McALESTER spouse of the late  ?  Ship Carpenter, Campbeltown who died ? .32.	Railed enclosure.  One stone and seven tablets.32.1	In memory of Ms FLORA WHITE and her four sisters, Ms BARBARA CAMPBELL and LILY, ELISABETH and MARY CAMPBELL also of their son GEORGE FORBES and of her daughter MARY WHITE who died 7 Feb 1876.32.2	Sacred to the memory of GEORGE MACNEAL Esq., of Ugadale who died 23 Feb 1861 in the 68th year of his age and of his wife MARY ELIZA LORING who died 25 Dec 1861 aged 59 years.32.3	HECTOR MACNEAL of Ugadale late Captain 79th (Queen’s Own Cameron Highrs), Deputy Lieutenant and Justice of the Peace for Argyll, born 10 Jul 1822, died 2 Oct 1905 and his wife CONSTANCE GLENCAIRN CAMPBELL, daughter of Colonel WALTER CAMPBELL of Skipness, born 16 Jul 1839, died 2 Jan 1912.32.4	TORQUIL MACNEAL of Ugadale, Deputy Lieutenant for Argyll T.D., J.P., born 6 Sep 1897, died 6 May 1973.32.5	HECTOR MACNEAL of Ugadale late Captain 92nd Gordon Highlanders, Deputy Lieutenant and J.P. for Argyll, Provost of Campbeltown, born 27 Dec 1862, died 25 May 1910 and his wife EDITH HELENA ROBERTSON, born 3 Jun 1867, died 19 Nov 1949.32.6	In memory of WALTER LORING MACNEAL second son of HECTOR MACNEAL of Ugadale and his wife CONSTANCE GLENCAIRN CAMPBELL who died and was buried at sea 26 May 1883 aged 18 years.32.7	Sacred to the memory of GEORGE FREDERICK MACNEAL Esq., who died 26 May 1871 aged 38, son of the late GEORGE MACNEAL Esq., of Ugadale and MARY ELIZA LORING his wife, JOHN LORING MACNEAL, born 2 May 1828 found drowned in the river Barwon, Geelong, Australia, 8 Sept 1855.32.8	Sacred to the memory of Captain JOHN NASH, Royal Navy, who died 14 Oct 1824 aged 56 years also MARY his wife who died 11 Dec 1839 aged 66 years.33.	Inscribed stoneErected by the family in loving memory of their dear mother and father MARY McLARDY BROWN, died 22 Aug 1922 in her 62nd years, DONALD SINCLAIR, died 18 Jan 1925 in his 70th year also their brother Pte. DUNCAN SINCLAIR, 8th A. & S.H. killed in action in France on 13 Nov 1916 aged 19 years, their brother DONALD who died 26 Dec 1945 aged 50 years, their sister FLORA, died 25 Feb 1950 aged 44 years.34.	Inscribed stoneErected by MARGRAT McLARTY in memory of her husband NEIL McCULASKY, Shipmaster in Campbeltown, who died 18 Feb 1795, aged 60 years.  Also lies here of his children DONALD, MARY, ROBERT, DONALD and FLORA who all died in infancy also the above MARGRAT McLARTY who died 17 Jan 1805 aged 58 years.35.	Railed enclosureIn memory of JAMES TAYLOR, builder who died 5 Nov 1847 aged 61 years and of ANNE McNAB his wife who died 5 Jan 1868 in the 80th year of her age also of their children, JAMES died 7 Feb 1849 aged 21 years, ANNE died 9 May 1849 aged 24 years, WILLIAM died 17 Jul 1851 aged 38 years, MARY died 12 Aug 1854 aged 38 years, ARCHIEBALD died 5 Feb 1857 aged 37 years, MARGARET died 9 Apr 1860 aged 38 years, CATHERINE born 6 June 1826 died 4 Jul 1899, DANIEL MACNAB the last surviving member of the family died 19 Mar 1903 aged 75 years. CATHERINE TAYLOR PLACE died 19 Feb 1857 aged 33 months.36. Inscribed stone, but broken in two and upside downSacred to the memory of  ELIZABETH HENWOOD wife of CHAS HENWOOD of the excise who died 4th Apr 1841 aged 27 years. “Forgive blest shade the tributary tear that mourns thy exit from a world like this.  Forgive the wish that would have kept thee here and staid thy progress to the realm of bliss”.  72. Inscribed stoneBe of good cheer for I believe God that it shall be even as it was told to me.Erected by EDWARD McTAGGART, flesher, Campbeltown and ISABELLA McALISTER his wife in memory of their sons JOHN and COLIN who died in infancy EDWARD aged 6½ years, DONALD aged 26 years, WILLIAM aged 25 years, EDWARD McTAGGART died 21 Dec 1875 aged 82 years, ISABELLA McALISTER a godfearing heroine of humble life died 26 May 1887 aged 80 years also their son JOHN who died 3 Jun 1923 aged 78 years.        Blessed Jesus was a favourite phrase       Fraught with solace in her dying days.        Words in substance often to him said       In life’s struggles in the sun and shade.       Quiet glory glistens through the gloom       Throwing shaded rays upon her tomb.       For she humbly long ere her decrease       Breathed the air of prayer, praise and peace.        Christ in you the hope of glory.Acts XXVII 25, Col II 27, Luke X 42.207. V.D.M. one of the ministers of the Collegiate Charge of the Parish of Campbeltown died 28 December 1843 in the 53 year of his age and 29 of his ministry, eighteen years of which he was pastor in the Parish of Southend he rendered signal literary service to the country as author of the history of the parish of Campbeltown for the Statistical Account of Scotland and as an ardent collector of ancient memoirs and legendary tales concerning Kintyre to be handed down to future ages.  His children are the 12th in descent from HENRY VII of England through AMELIA SOPHIA STANLEY (the Mona’s Queen  who was mother of their ancestor WILLIAM 2nd Lord Nairn and also of CHARLES lst Earl of Dunmore and JOHN, lst Duke of ATHOL.808.2	In memory of the children of Rev.
